<span style="font-size:36px;"><span style="color: rgb(255, 240, 245); font-weight: bold;">Eye of the Owl - Hieronymus Bosch VR</span></span>

<div class="lp-element lp-pom-text nlh" id="lp-pom-text-2462" style="height: auto;">
<p class="lplh-45">
<span style="font-family:open sans;"><span style="font-size: 22px;">Hieronymus Bosch lived and died in the Netherlands about 500 Years ago. &nbsp;His work is known for its bizarre imagery and detailed landscapes. <br>
<br>In this documentary style VR experience you can examine the painting in intimate detail while visiting H Boschs &nbsp;studio where he created the masterpiece over 500 years ago.</span></span>
</p>
</div>
<div class="lp-element lp-pom-text nlh" id="lp-pom-text-2464" style="height: auto;">
<p class="lplh-45" style="text-align: center;">
<span style="font-size: 36px;"><span style="font-family: oswald;">Taking the viewer back to the 15th century Netherlands to meet Hieronymus Bosch and intimately behold his masterpiece <br>The Garden of Earthly Delights.</span></span>
</p>
</div>
<div class="lp-element lp-pom-text nlh" id="lp-pom-text-2468" style="height: auto;">
<p class="lplh-45" style="text-align: center;">
<span style="font-size:44px;"><span style="font-family:oswald;">The 50th Anniversary of Apollo 17!</span></span><span style="font-family:open sans;"><span style="font-size:28px;">
<br>Launched July 2019:</span></span>
<br>
<span style="font-family:open sans;"><span style="font-size:28px;">Celebrate by taking a ride in the classic Lunar Rover!</span></span>
</p>
<p class="lplh-38" style="text-align: center;">
<span style="font-family:open sans;"><span style="font-size:28px;">As the world celebrates the 50th anniversary of the Apollo moon landings, Moonbuggy VR is the perfect way to delve deeper into the manned moon expeditions and really experience what it was like to be on the moon and drive the classic rover.</span></span>
</p>
